# C64 Commander Prod Hardening 8 Worklog

Run started: 2026-06-05T23:53:04+01:00

## Coverage hang fix 2026-06-15 (ConfigBrowserPage infinite re-render loop)

- 2026-06-15T23:29:00+01:00 - Resumed the "Android coverage build hang" investigation on `fix/hardening-3` (head `e9bdc85b`). `npm run test:coverage` (`scripts/run-unit-coverage.mjs`, 45 sequential Vitest batches) hung indefinitely; CI seen still running after 1h28m. Prior handover had bisected the hang to chunk 6 "half-B" (7 files) and was about to split further.
- 2026-06-15T23:30:00+01:00 - Continued bisection: Group C (first 3 of half-B) hung (exit 124). Ran the 3 individually — `tests/unit/lib/lighting/capabilities.test.ts` and `tests/unit/lib/snapshot/snapshotFiltering.test.ts` passed; `tests/unit/pages/ConfigBrowserPage.test.tsx` HUNG on its own. Isolated the culprit file.
- 2026-06-15T23:32:00+01:00 - Reproduced the hang WITHOUT coverage too, so it is not a v8-instrumentation issue. Confirmed it is the source, not the test: the test file was unchanged in `e9bdc85b`, but `src/pages/ConfigBrowserPage.tsx` was (74 ins / 18 del, the BUG-033 re-sync work). Checking out the parent's `ConfigBrowserPage.tsx` made all 20 tests pass and exit cleanly; restoring HEAD's version re-hung.
- 2026-06-15T23:33:00+01:00 - Characterised the wedge: a backgrounded run pegged the Vitest worker at ~106% CPU (synchronous/runaway loop, not an idle open handle). Also reaped orphaned tinypool worker children left spinning by earlier `timeout`-killed runs (`timeout` kills the parent Vitest, not the fork child).
- 2026-06-15T23:34:00+01:00 - Localised to the new code path: all four Reset/Refresh tests ("resets audio mixer to defaults", "shows no-op toast when audio mixer is already at defaults", "reports audio mixer reset failures", "refreshes category data") hang individually; these are exactly the tests that drive `resyncPendingRef`.
- 2026-06-15T23:40:00+01:00 - ROOT CAUSE: the new snapshot-effect branch `if (resyncPendingRef.current) { syncAudioConfiguredItems(items); }` feeds `items` straight into `setAudioConfiguredItems`. `items` is rebuilt by `extractConfigItems` whenever `categoryData` changes identity; the `mockUseC64Category` mock returns a fresh object every render, so `items` is a new reference each render. The effect lists `items` as a dep → setState(new ref) → re-render → effect re-runs → ... an infinite synchronous re-render loop for the whole `resyncPendingRef === true` (Reset/Refresh await) window, starving the event loop so the awaited promises never settle and Vitest's test timeout (event-loop based) never fires. The old code fed the *stable* `soloSnapshotRef.current`, so React bailed out — no loop. (In production react-query's structural sharing keeps `data`/`items` referentially stable, so the device itself never looped; the loop is exposed only by referentially-unstable upstreams.)
- 2026-06-15T23:44:00+01:00 - FIX 1 (root cause): added module-level `configListItemsEqual(a, b)` (per-item serialized compare; `details` is flat/JSON-safe) and made `syncAudioConfiguredItems` bail when the next items are value-equal to `audioConfiguredRef.current`. Breaks the loop (React stops re-rendering once content matches) while preserving the BUG-033 intent (genuinely-changed items are still adopted). Hardens the component against any referentially-unstable upstream.
- 2026-06-15T23:45:00+01:00 - FIX 2 (latent NPE the hang had masked): `resetAudioMixer`/`handleRefresh` read `refreshed.data` from `await refetch()`, but the test mocks `refetch: vi.fn()` → `undefined` → `TypeError: Cannot read properties of undefined (reading 'data')`. Made both sites `refreshed?.data` (extractConfigItems already treats undefined as `[]`); production react-query always returns a result object, so behaviour is unchanged there.
- 2026-06-15T23:45:42+01:00 - VERIFIED: `tests/unit/pages/ConfigBrowserPage.test.tsx` now 20/20 pass, no hang (3.26s, no coverage). With coverage, the chunk-6 "half-B" group (6 jsdom files; `generatePlayAssets` runs in unit-node) is 90/90 in 11.4s. ESLint + Prettier clean on the changed file. Full `npm run test:coverage` launched to completion as the final gate.

- 2026-06-11T23:36 Candidate ranking (rubric in PLANS.md): A=19, E=15, B=14, C=10, D=9. Selected **Candidate A** (Pixel P5 auto-advance discrepancy). Core anomaly: P5 best-effort `demo.sid` stayed at elapsed `0:00` for the full 35 s window (vs P2 `10_Orbyte.sid` advancing 0:00->0:04 within seconds), no toast, then deterministic auto-advance suites passed. Hypothesis class: playback never started (local-fixture item start failure or automation click not landing), so the auto-advance timer was never armed — not an auto-advance logic failure. Assumption to verify against evidence artifact `docs/plans/hardening/1/artifacts/deep-hil/p5-auto-advance-current.json`: whether a sidplay/run request was actually issued.
- Stop criteria: verdict + causal model + >=3 invariants recorded; handoff sequence if window <25% with work remaining.
- 2026-06-11T23:38 Candidate A causal analysis (static): P5 evidence artifact `deep-hil/p5-auto-advance-current.json` shows `playClicked: true`, elapsed pinned at 0:00, remaining normalized -0:29 -> -0:30 (consistent with `setElapsedMs(0)`/`setDurationMs` at usePlaybackController.ts:741-742 running), `finalPause: false`, `toasts: []`. Code proof: every throw path out of the start chain reaches `reportUserError` via `handlePlay`/`startPlaylist`/`flushPendingUserSkip` catches, and destructive toasts never auto-dismiss (`use-toast.ts:214-215` dismisses non-destructive only). Therefore a thrown start error cannot produce the observed no-toast state; the observation is only consistent with (a) a never-settling await in the start chain (un-timeboxed `FolderPicker.readFile[FromTree]` native SAF read, `toBlob`, or metadata resolution), (b) a start superseded by a routing change (suppressed by policy), or (c) the automation click not dispatching.
- 2026-06-11T23:42 Device probe 1+2 (CDP, u64): forwarded WebView devtools (pid 9290). Probe accidentally targeted per-row `Play 10_Orbyte.sid` control; both runs started playback successfully (elapsed 0:00->0:13 advancing, Pause enabled, no toasts), paused at 14 s to stay clear of the 30 s auto-advance boundary. Key recovered evidence: the oldest retained app-log entries (buffer cap 500) were from the exact original P5 minute (21:40:46Z) and showed connection churn during P5: `Connection switched to real device`, `Discovery probe request failed`, `C64 API request superseded by routing change`, `C64 API request failure ignored after routing change`. P5's own `Playback request started` trail had already rotated out of the buffer.
- 2026-06-11T23:45 Candidate A verdict: playback start and auto-advance arming verified healthy on current build/device (3 successful starts; watchdog armed). Original P5 anomaly NOT reproduced; most probable cause is a playback start superseded by the concurrent routing change at 21:40:46Z, whose rejection is policy-suppressed (no toast for superseded operations) — leaving a silently dead user Play click. Residual question recorded for continuation: whether a background routing change superseding a foreground user action should retry or surface feedback (policy tension between ERROR_POLICY §3 suppression and §2 foreground-feedback guarantee).
- 2026-06-11T23:46 USER REDIRECT (binding): user identified that the SID was played such that the device did not know its true length; required root-cause + fix so the SID is sent as REST payload with length attached. Filed BUG-019.

- 2026-06-12T00:02 Superseded-foreground-start feedback implemented (Candidate A residual #1, filed BUG-020): `reportUserError` has no abort suppression, so a play start superseded by a routing change either raised a destructive `Playback failed: Aborted` toast (false alarm) or, when the rejection escaped the chain, nothing at all (the silent P5 state; P5 window logs contained `Ignored abort-like unhandled rejection`). Added `reportPlaybackStartFailure` in `usePlaybackController.ts`: abort-like start failures (via canonical `isAbortLikeError` from `requestRuntime.ts`) now report a non-destructive S2 notice "Playback interrupted / The connection changed while starting playback. Press Play again." at all three user-start catch sites (`handlePlay`, `startPlaylist`, `flushPendingUserSkip`); non-abort failures keep the destructive default. Background suppression untouched.
- 2026-06-12T00:04 Bounded local reads implemented (Candidate A residual #2, part of BUG-020): `fileLibraryUtils.ts` lazy wrappers now bound `FolderPicker.readFile`/`readFileFromTree` with a 15 s timeout that rejects with the established "Local file unavailable. Re-add it to the playlist." message, so a never-settling native SAF read can no longer hold `playStartInFlightRef` and permanently block `playTransitionQueueRef` with zero feedback.

- 2026-06-13T10:38+01:00 Root cause (source): `backgroundExecutionManager.ts` module-global refcount `activeCount` (native `stop()` only at 0); `PlayFilesPage.tsx` `backgroundExecutionActiveRef = useRef(false)`. The P1-6 unmount-while-playing path (lines 561-596) keeps background execution active WITHOUT decrementing; on remount the fresh ref=false makes the start effect call `startBackgroundExecution` again -> activeCount=2; later Stop decrements 2->1 only, so native stop/wake-lock release never runs. The refcount is intentional (its unit test enshrines it); the bug is the unmount(keep)/remount(start) asymmetry. Filed BUG-025 (distinct JS root cause; BUG-024 native `updateDueAt(null)` guard intact per `09:16:19 "Not running — ignoring dueAt clear request"`).
- 2026-06-13T10:40+01:00 Fix implemented: exported `isBackgroundExecutionActive()` from `backgroundExecutionManager.ts`; `PlayFilesPage.tsx` now `useRef(isBackgroundExecutionActive())` so a remounted Play page ADOPTS the active session instead of re-incrementing. Added regression tests to `tests/unit/lib/native/backgroundExecutionManager.test.ts`. Focused validation: `npx vitest run tests/unit/lib/native/backgroundExecutionManager.test.ts tests/unit/pages/playFiles/backgroundExecutionPolicy.test.ts tests/unit/pages/playFiles/PlayFilesPage.featureFlagContracts.test.ts` (18 passed) and `npx tsc --noEmit --pretty false` (exit 0). Change left UNCOMMITTED in working tree for user review (per repo commit policy). Rebuilding/redeploying for HIL re-validation next.

Contrast with the pre-fix build where the identical scenario left size=1 indefinitely (2 repros). `WakeLock acquired/released` confirmed emitted by native `BackgroundExecutionService.kt:283/292` (mirrored to JS log store): pre-fix the refcount was pinned >=1 so the manager's `activeCount>1` guard suppressed native start/stop (one continuous lock -> leak after Stop); post-fix the refcount oscillates 0<->1 so native start/stop fire each transition and the final Stop reaches 0 -> native stop -> release. Fix mechanism confirmed.

Could not complete the reconciliation/Refresh self-heal test because c64u dropped out (below). Host curl `/v1/info` → exit 56 / HTTP 000 (immediate refuse), confirming a device-level REST/network dropout, not an app bug. The app's degradation reporting is ACCURATE (no false-positive, no silent failure) — a positive for Product Standard #6. Per c64u traffic policy I stopped escalating; one gentle re-probe after a quiet gap still HTTP 000 — needs more quiet (self-clears per memory). ### BUG-028 (NEW, Medium) — discovered, root-caused, FIXED, validated
- Symptom: after the first-iteration BUG-027 fix, a Capacitor `backButton` listener is registered at startup on a fresh Home (no overlay) and never removed → Android Back consumed (no-op Escape) instead of Capacitor default. Evidence: fresh-Home logcat `addListener backButton` (participant build, 16:04), and diagnostics export logged `"Android Back dismissed topmost interstitial"` on a no-overlay Back (14:48:53Z) with TabBar visible (modal `stack` empty ⇒ leaked `popoverBackDismissCount>0`).
- Oracle correction: `dumpsys mCurrentFocus` is NOT a valid trap oracle — the ORIGINAL pre-BUG-027 build (built+installed from stash; ZERO backButton listeners at fresh Home, verified by empty logcat) ALSO kept focus on `.MainActivity` after Back (Capacitor default `webView.goBack()`). Real oracle = interstitial-handler diagnostics log + logcat listener add/remove balance.
- Root cause: `usePopoverBackDismiss()` was called in each Radix `*Content` wrapper body. Those wrappers render for the whole lifetime of their parent; and Radix `Select.Content` (node_modules @radix-ui/react-select: `if(!context.open) return createPortal(<div>{children}</div>, fragment)`) renders children into an off-screen DocumentFragment even while CLOSED → hook registered permanently whenever any `<Select>` was mounted (every page). The participant-in-Content fix fixed dropdown/popover/context (Presence-gated) but NOT Select.
- Fix: `usePopoverBackDismissRoot({open,defaultOpen,onOpenChange})` (interstitial-state.tsx) tracks the Radix Root's logical open state and registers only while open; `Select`/`DropdownMenu`/`Popover`/`ContextMenu` Root wrappers spread it; participants removed from all 4 Content components.
- Validation (final Root-level build, offline): (a) fresh Home logcat = NO backButton listener (vs participant build which leaked one here) — Select-closed no longer registers ✅; (b) Diagnostics dialog open → `addListener` (56809308); Android Back → ONE notify → `removeListener` — clean, no leak ✅; (c) Diagnostics `⋮` dropdown nested over dialog → Back dismissed overlays + returned to page, NO route pop ✅. Offline `GET /v1/info Failed to fetch` errors correctly surfaced as Problems (not silent). No crashes/exceptions/StrictMode in package logcat.
- Minor OBSERVATION (pre-existing, Low, NOT my change): a single Android Back over a dropdown nested INSIDE a dialog collapses BOTH layers (synthetic-Escape reaches both Radix DismissableLayers) rather than only the topmost; harmless (returns to page, no route loss). Same in first-fix; out of BUG-027/028 scope.

### Carry-forward / cleanup
- Both devices DOWN → standalone `/disks` + `/config` Select & dropdown Back must be re-validated on the FINAL Root-level build when a device recovers (preserved by construction — Root fix changes only registration timing, not the Back→Escape dismiss). c64u UltiSID/Vol-Socket-1 → 0 dB cleanup STILL BLOCKED (c64u down). No device writes made this loop; nothing to restore.
- Code changed: yes (5 ui files). Build/deploy: yes (`npm run build && npx cap sync android && ./gradlew assembleDebug`, installed via droidmind). Tests/coverage: none. droidmind: yes; c64scope/c64bridge: no.
- VERDICT #33: **FIXED** — BUG-027 (overlay Android Back) FIXED+validated; BUG-028 (back-listener leak / Back trap) discovered+root-caused+FIXED+validated. Fix uncommitted (ready for commit/review). Continuation: Ralph Robin.

- 2026-06-13T16:54+01:00 VERDICT #36: **FIXED** — Settings connection/diagnostics/persistence probe pack found and fixed BUG-029 (Diagnostics Share all writes the ZIP but records an in-app export error when Android Share returns canceled). Root cause: `diagnosticsExport.ts` treated every Capacitor `Share.share` rejection as an error; Android returns a plain `{ message: "Share canceled" }` object on user/platform cancel, so the first fix that handled only `Error` still left a raw diagnostics error. Final fix handles both shapes as non-error cancellation after the ZIP is written; real failures still log/rethrow. Build/deploy: `./build --skip-tests --install-apk --device-id 9B081FFAZ001WX` twice during refinement; final installed package `versionName=0.8.7-rc3-9ba1c`, `lastUpdateTime=2026-06-13 16:52:45`. Focused regression: `npx vitest run tests/unit/lib/diagnostics/diagnosticsExport.test.ts` passed 18/18 after both edits. Coverage not run (HIL loop; user did not request coverage).

Added `describeUnhandledRejectionReason()` so structured plugin payloads log `Share canceled` instead of `[object Object]`. Focused regression added in `tests/unit/App.runtime.test.tsx` for a structured `{ message: "Share canceled" }` rejection.

- 2026-06-13T17:56+01:00 FIX LOOP RESULT: BUG-029 is now **FIXED** on the current build `0.8.7-rc3-4c093`. #38 first reproduced that the Settings Diagnostics card remained a weak entry point under droidmind, but the app-bar status badge reliably opened Diagnostics. Live probe pack evidence showed the chooser-cancel symptom still existed after the #37 `App.tsx` patch: `Share all` wrote a valid ZIP and opened the Android chooser, but after chooser Back/cancel the live Problems list showed `ERROR {"message":"Share canceled"}` even though package logcat had no `DIAGNOSTICS_EXPORT`/`Diagnostics share failed`. Root cause narrowed to the global `console.error` diagnostics bridge in `src/lib/diagnostics/logger.ts`, which was still forwarding user-cancellation payloads into Diagnostics as console-originated errors. Patched the bridge to suppress forwarding when `classifyError(firstArg).failureClass === "user-cancellation"`. Added focused regression `tests/unit/diagnostics/logger.test.ts` covering `console.error({ message: "Share canceled" })`; targeted test passed 25/25 and Prettier check passed. Rebuilt/redeployed with `./build --skip-tests --install-apk --device-id 9B081FFAZ001WX`, then reran the exact HIL path one-for-one: Home app-bar badge -> Diagnostics -> overflow -> `Share all` -> chooser visible -> Android Back cancel -> return to Diagnostics. ZIP `cache/c64commander-diagnostics-all-2026-06-13-1655-03Z.zip` was written, pulled, and unpacked to `docs/agentic/artifacts/iter38/diagnostics/export-165503/`. Final live Problems view after cancel showed only expected offline `/v1/info` failures; there was NO fresh `ERROR {"message":"Share canceled"}`, `DIAGNOSTICS_EXPORT`, or `Diagnostics share failed` entry in the current 17:55 validation window, and package-filtered logcat stayed clean for the same signatures. Historical `Share canceled` entries are still present inside the exported diagnostics files because those exports intentionally include prior stored logs; they are not fresh runtime failures from the fixed validation pass.

## Ralph loop iteration — 2026-06-13 #43 (Claude — resolve remaining BUG-031 auto-rotation checkbox half)

- Startup 2026-06-13T19:11+01:00: branch `fix/hardening-2` @ `389af951`; source identity `0.8.7-rc3-389af`. Rebuilt+reinstalled this loop (`./build --skip-tests --install-apk --device-id 9B081FFAZ001WX`, exit 0); droidmind `get_app_info` = `0.8.7-rc3-389af`, Running, so current-build HIL claims are valid AND the uncommitted BUG-031 fix is guaranteed in the APK.
- Capacity checkpoint: Ralph Robin provider `claude`, usable 5h 94% / weekly 83% => `>=40%` band. HIL peers: droidmind yes; mobile-mcp yes; c64scope exposed; c64bridge VICE-backed only. First-touch/pre-action blocker: none.
- Previous verdict: #42 `DEFECT` (theme fixed, auto-rotation checkbox still DEFECT_OPEN). Selected family this loop: **Settings Appearance / auto-rotation checkbox resolution** with mandatory diagnostics/log sweep.
- Targeted validation before HIL: `npm run test -- tests/unit/pages/SettingsPage.test.tsx` -> PASS (62/62, includes the touch-pointerUp regression tests).

- Root-cause investigation (this context window): compared `src/components/ui/button.tsx` (working touch bridge) vs `src/components/ui/checkbox.tsx` (#41 staged bridge). Button's `onPointerUp` calls the `onClick` *callback* directly + `suppressNextClickRef` skips the natural click's callback → action fires once. Checkbox's `onPointerUp` dispatched a synthetic DOM `element.click()`; Radix Root toggles internally on EVERY click, so synthetic click + natural touch-click = two toggles = net no change. Idempotent `setTheme()` masked it on theme buttons; a toggle is not idempotent.
- Pre-fix HIL proof (installed bridge APK `0.8.7-rc3-389af`): tap1 unchecked→checked (1 net toggle); tap2 checked→checked (0 net). Diagnostics Actions trace of tap2 showed TWO `click auto-rotation`+`toggle` pairs (.402/.403 [false] and .440/.441 [true]) = double-fire confirmed. Nondeterministic single-vs-double across taps.
- Fix: removed the synthetic-click bridge from `checkbox.tsx` (plain Radix checkbox; global pointer-up model supplies the flash for `[role="checkbox"]`). Updated `tests/unit/pages/SettingsPage.test.tsx` to simulate the real touch sequence (`pointerUp`+`click`) asserting one net toggle per tap. `npm run test -- tests/unit/pages/SettingsPage.test.tsx` PASS 62/62; `npx prettier --check` PASS. Rebuilt+reinstalled (`./build --skip-tests --install-apk --device-id 9B081FFAZ001WX`, BUILD SUCCESSFUL, Success); droidmind `get_app_info` = `0.8.7-rc3-389af` Running (new install-path hash; bundle `index-CSCBpaNa.js`).

### #48 consolidated evidence — Diagnostics overflow-menu dismissal (BUG-032 found + fixed + HIL-validated)

Probe family: global app-shell **Diagnostics dialog + overflow "Views" popover + nested Android-Back dismissal layering**. Target u64 · U64E HEALTHY (192.168.1.13, fw 3.14e); UI-only family, no c64u traffic. Current build verified: source `0.8.7-rc3-c0396` == installed (`get_app_info`).

**Defect found — BUG-032 (Medium): diagnostics overflow "Views" menu is a hand-rolled `<div>` (DiagnosticsDialog.tsx) that never joined the Radix dismissal layer stack.** Two deterministic symptoms on the pre-fix build:
- Android Back with the menu open closed the ENTIRE Diagnostics dialog (not just the menu). Root cause: the InterstitialStateProvider back handler dispatches one Escape keydown on `document`; the only registered dismiss participant is the AppSheet (Radix `Dialog`) `DismissableLayer`, so its bubble-phase handler dismissed the dialog and the unregistered panel unmounted with it. Logcat confirmed exactly ONE `Capacitor/AppPlugin: backButton` per press → one Escape closing two surfaces. Repro 2/2.
- Outside tap neither dismissed the menu NOR was absorbed: it fell through to the underlying activity row and toggled it (chevron `>`→`v`). Root cause: no `onInteractOutside`/backdrop on the bare panel.
- CONTRAST (isolation): Back on the Latency secondary view (a real Radix `AppSheet` layer) correctly returned to the main Diagnostics view — Radix-managed layers dismiss correctly; only the hand-rolled panel was broken.

**Fix:** wrap the overflow panel in Radix `DismissableLayer` (`asChild`, `disableOutsidePointerEvents`, `onFocusOutside`→preventDefault, `onDismiss`→close). It now shares the dialog's `DismissableLayer` context as the topmost layer, so Radix's `isHighestLayer` guard (dist line 98-99) closes ONLY the menu on Back/Escape (the dialog defers), and `disableOutsidePointerEvents` dismisses+absorbs outside taps. `asChild` preserves the existing two-profile markup/positioning. First aborted attempt (capture-phase Escape `stopImmediatePropagation`) was discarded after HIL: an Escape dispatched ON `document` fires all document listeners in registration order at the target phase (capture flag ignored), so Radix's earlier-registered handler still ran first — the layer-stack `isHighestLayer` mechanism is the only correct fix.

**Post-fix HIL validation (current build, rebuilt+reinstalled+relaunched):**
- Back with menu open → ONLY menu closes, dialog stays. Deterministic 2/2.
- Second Back → dialog closes (correct second-layer dismissal).
- Outside tap (250,1700) → menu dismisses AND is absorbed; underlying `/v1/info` row chevron unchanged (`>`), no pass-through.
- Overflow menu items still actuate inside the layer: "Clear all" opened its nested Radix `AlertDialog` ("Clear diagnostics?"); Cancel closed it and diagnostics were NOT cleared (Filters 72 of 72) and the menu correctly stayed open — nested AlertDialog fully compatible.

| Action ID | Route/Page | UI element | User operation | Expected | ≈200ms | ≈1s/effect | Oracle | Latency | Diagnostics/log | Status | Artifacts | Cleanup |

### #86 consolidated evidence — version identity fix + Disks selector/dialog/filter UI pack on current APK

Build/deploy setup found a real source-version defect before HIL could be current-build: native package identity became `0.8.8-rc1-37f0e`, but the Home System Info row still showed `App 0.8.7-rc3`. Pixel` present; `lsusb -v -d 18d1:4eea` shows ONLY `bInterfaceClass 1 Audio` (MIDI function) interfaces — the ADB/vendor interface is not exposed. ⇒ The Pixel is in MIDI USB mode, so adb (and therefore droidmind/mobile-mcp) cannot bind it. This is not fixable from the host without ADB or physical screen access (chicken-and-egg).

- NO-HIL-PEER fix exception checked: only Low-severity defects open (BUG-030 dev-only Radix aria warning stripped from prod APK; BUG-022 SAF startup diagnostic). No safe high-value no-HIL root-cause fix for a blocker/high/medium defect exists ⇒ no code change this loop (a documentation-only or coverage loop is forbidden).

## Ralph loop iteration #71 (2026-06-15, Claude) — Settings connection/diagnostics/persistence family + BUG-035 FIX

**Build identity:** parent `d05c7a7a` → **committed BUG-035+BUG-037 as `472b2c75`**; rebuilt+reinstalled twice; final installed APK `0.8.7-rc3-472b2` == committed HEAD == resolve-version == get_app_info → **current-build HIL VALID, stale-label ambiguity ENDED**. c64u 192.168.1.167 DOWN (HTTP 000) entire loop; u64 192.168.1.13 HEALTHY (HTTP 200). Capacity claude 5h 49% (>=40% band, min 8 / target 12-20).

**BUG-035 root cause (confirmed on-device, then fixed):** About/Home version showed `0.7.9-rc1` (package.json) while Git ID `d05c7a7a` / native APK `0.8.7-rc3-d05c7`. Root cause = `resolveBuildVersionLabel` (src/lib/versionLabel.ts:66-73) only trusts the generated `src/version.ts` label when its release base matches the package.json base; generated base `0.8.7` ≠ package base `0.7.9` → guard discarded the generated label and fell back to package.json `0.7.9-rc1`. Native versionName uses resolve-version.sh directly (no guard) → diverged. **Fix:** bump package.json `version` 0.7.9-rc1 → 0.8.7-rc3 (the release tag base). After fix, base `0.8.7`==`0.8.7` → guard passes → in-app version = `0.8.7-rc3-<sha>`, matching native. Validated on Home SystemInfo AND Settings About on both rebuilds (`d05c7`, then committed `472b2`).

### Consolidated CTA evidence (current build `d05c7`, then validation on committed `472b2`)
| Action ID | Route/Page | UI element | User operation | Expected | ≈200ms | ≈1s/effect | Oracle | Latency | Diag/log | Status | Artifacts | Cleanup |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|

- **CONFIRMED c64u mount mechanism (resolves long-standing "FtpClient host=192.168.1.13 during c64u op" open question, ledger Play rows #22/#24):** mounting a u64-origin disk on c64u = `FtpClient.readFile host=192.168.1.13` (the disk's ORIGIN host, u64) → `POST /v1/drives/a:mount?type=d64&mode=readwrite` with the d64 BYTES as body → c64u stores at `/Temp/tempNNNN` (index increments per mount: temp0000→temp0001). This is correct source attribution (disk imported from u64's /USB2), NOT a stale-target bug. Contrast u64 (#32): mount-by-PATH (PUT `a:mount?image=<path>`, no body) since the file is local to u64.
- **OBS-A (Low, NEW candidate, cosmetic/UX):** On c64u the mounted-drive card shows the device temp path `/.../temp0000` instead of the friendly disk name "Boulder Dash 2.d64" shown on u64 (#32). Device state correct; label less recognizable to a user (can't tell which disk is mounted). App-side cosmetic; could map device temp file → originating disk name in the drive card label.
- **OBS-B (latency note, not a defect):** c64u disk mount = ~1080-1102ms (the single over-budget latencySample, 1102ms). Inherent: it uploads the ~170KB d64 (FTP read from u64 + HTTP POST body). u64 mount-by-path was 911ms (#32). Long-op data-transfer semantics; eject/reset/power all 35-260ms (well under budget). Consider explicit busy/progress indicator during the ~1s mount upload.

The 1581 commit failed ONLY because c64u dropped out (infra), not an app fault.
- **PRIMARY DEFECT — BUG-041 CONFIRMED + STRENGTHENED (stale HEALTHY badge):** While c64u was fully unreachable (HTTP 000) for ~3+ min and every REST request failed, the global health badge stayed green **"C64U HEALTHY"** the entire time. Diagnostics health card read **"Last check 49m 38s ago"**. ZIP `healthHistory` has only **3 entries** — `17:11:54Z` Unhealthy, **`17:40:58Z` Healthy** (durationMs 2651 = #82 recovery; this stale entry drove the badge), `18:31:19Z` Unhealthy (my manual check). **No health check ran for ~50 min (17:40→18:31Z)** despite the mid-session dropout and many `rest.get` failures → confirms health is refreshed ONLY by explicit triggers (launch/foreground/manual), is **NOT periodic**, and is **NOT invalidated by observed REST request failures**. Manual "Run health check" correctly flipped the badge to Unhealthy (REST Timeout 3000ms; dependent probes cleanly cancelled). User-facing impact: a reassuring green HEALTHY badge while the device is completely down and every action fails. Fix candidates: (a) TTL on persisted health, (b) invalidate/degrade health after N consecutive `C64U_HTTP_FAILURE` (the app already has the failure events), (c) periodic background health check. Borderline Medium given the misleading-during-active-failures impact.
- **Two NON-defects confirmed (resilience working as intended):** (1) the duplicate Drive-Type→1581 PUT is an intentional **retry-once on Connection reset** (`Drive config update retry`), idempotent config write, then graceful give-up with accurate inline error — sound. (2) the `TypeError: Failed to fetch` Problem is the standard WebView network-failure representation (`transient:true`, host unreachable), correctly caught and logged with full context — not a code bug.
- **c64u DROPOUT (incident, logged C64U_INCIDENTS.md):** c64u went unreachable at ~18:26Z during the Drive Type→1581 config write and did not recover this loop (probes HTTP 000, then 4s timeouts). First failure was `Connection reset` on a 47s-idle keep-alive socket (network-layer), escalating to `Host unreachable`. Trigger correlated with the 1581 write, BUT: (i) the 1571 write 47s earlier (also a mode change/drive reinit) succeeded cleanly; (ii) load was a single tiny config PUT (cannot "overload" c64u); (iii) [[c64u-flakiness]] documents intermittent firmware dropouts. → Attributed to **c64u firmware flakiness, NOT app-induced degradation**; app pacing was minimal and correct. Per the dropout-pivot rule, did NOT end early: pivoted to diagnostics-mining (confirmed clean app dropout handling: accurate inline error, retry-once, no false-positive foreground success, no silent failure — only gap is BUG-041 badge staleness) + exhausted the UI-only Diagnostics family.
- **DEVICE LOG sweep:** (1) PID-logcat (cleared at start, PID 19509) `iter84/logcat/` — **0 FATAL/ANR/crash/StrictMode/Chromium-error**; the only E lines are `Capacitor/Plugin: Connection reset` (SocketException/ConnectionResetException) for the 1581 write + `C64U_HTTP_FAILURE` (Connection reset → Host unreachable) for the failed config write + background polls — ALL attributed to the c64u dropout, none unexplained. `drivetype-failure.log` preserves the full failure trace (buffer later rolled). ## Ralph loop iteration #88 (2026-06-17, Claude/Opus) — BUG-040 FIXED + HIL-validated

**Family:** Play background-execution / lifecycle (top open Medium, BUG-040). **Build:** `0.8.8-rc1-37f0e` (HEAD `37f0eeff`); fix in `src/pages/PlayFilesPage.tsx` (uncommitted), rebuilt+reinstalled. **Peers:** droidmind (all UI), CDP/WebView devtools (sessionStorage reads, root-cause), dumpsys power/oom + package logcat (wake-lock oracle), direct REST `http://c64u/v1/...` (UltiSID read-back/restore). c64u HEALTHY throughout (fw 1.1.0 id 5D4E12). c64scope not used (wake-lock lifecycle, not A/V). **Capacity:** >=40% band; ~16 droidmind product actions + lifecycle keyevents; adversarial transitions: nav-away-while-playing, background-from-non-Play-route, background-from-Play (control), Pause/Resume, Android Back ×2.

**Root cause (CDP+logcat proven):** Play→Home nav produces TWO bg-exec teardowns: real instance unmounts isPlaying=true → KEEPS lock (logs "Leaving background playback guard active"); a transient PlayFilesPage instance (mounted during SwipeNavigation transition, adopts active session via `isBackgroundExecutionActive()` but isPlaying=false before async session restore) then STOPS the native FGS → `WakeLock released`. Persisted `c64u_playback_session:v1` was `isPlaying:true` while `dumpsys power=size=0` — BUG-025 sibling (premature stop by transient adopter).

**Fix:** `hasObservedActivePlaybackRef` — only an instance that has itself observed `isPlaying===true` may release bg-exec (main stop effect + unmount cleanup early-return when false, keeping the adopted flag so no double-start). Transient adopters never release the live lock.

**Root cause and fix:** Capacitor Android retained the `Share.share` call in `Bridge.pluginCallForLastActivity`; after chooser cancel, `BridgeActivity.onSaveInstanceState` tried to persist it and `SharePlugin.saveInstanceState()` returned null, producing the `E Capacitor` line. `MainActivity.onSaveInstanceState` now clears only pending `Share/share` activity calls before delegating to Capacitor. Other pending activity calls are left intact.

Post-fix `postfix-cycle1.log` and `postfix-cycle2-close-before-home.log` each had 0 old Share state-save errors and 1 targeted `D MainActivity: Cleared unpersistable Share activity call before state save`. Final package log `iter96/logcat/final-package.log`: 71 app-PID lines, V=21 D=44 I=2 W=2 E=0 F=0; no crash/ANR/fatal/StrictMode/AndroidRuntime. ### #117 verdict: `DEFECT` (BUG-052 reproduced) + `RALPH ROBIN CONTINUATION READY`

- BUG-053 long-read pack: 3 Audio Mixer open/close cycles + final open completed on Pixel 4 build `0.8.8-rc1-1fd46` via u64 IP `192.168.1.13`. `droidmind_cta_action_count=18`. Health badge stayed `● Healthy · u64 · U64E` across the entire pack. Health-check overall 1732ms; latency p50 44ms / p90 63ms / p99 319ms. No Audio Mixer request over 60ms. Max latency sample 319ms (Telnet/Other); 4 samples over 200ms (230, 245, 217, 319) — all well under #113's multi-second outliers. BUG-053 did NOT reproduce on u64 IP.
- BUG-052 reproduced live: typed hostname `u64` into Settings Connection, tapped Save & Connect. Logcat shows the full chain: `MdnsResolver.resolve({"host":"u64","timeoutMs":1500})` → `System DNS lookup failed for u64.local` (5s wait) → `System DNS lookup failed for u64` → app pushes raw plugin error `{"save":false,"callbackId":"...","pluginId":"MdnsResolver","methodName":"resolve","success":false,"error":{"message":"Cannot resolve host 'u64' via mDNS"}}` → app then attempts `http://u64/v1/info` direct HTTP → fails with `Unable to resolve host "u64"`. Badge transitions correctly to `Offline, device not reachable`, but the raw plugin error object is what reaches the JS layer — no app-side contextualization or safe-mode guidance.
- Diagnostics ZIP pulled and analyzed: `docs/agentic/artifacts/iter117/diagnostics/c64commander-diagnostics-all-2026-06-18-0635-10Z.zip`. Counts: logs 500, error-logs 0, actions 178, traces 740, latencySamples 71. Health snapshot Healthy/Online, problemCount 0, lastRestActivity `GET /v1/configs/Audio Mixer 200`. Probes: REST 107ms, FTP 70ms, TELNET 319ms, CONFIG 809ms, RASTER 88ms, JIFFY 266ms.
- Package-filtered logcat: no crash/FATAL/ANR/StrictMode. `MdnsResolverPlugin` resolver-attempt lines + raw plugin-error JSON pushed to JS confirm BUG-052 root cause is the JS layer treating `MdnsResolver.resolve` failure as a transparent raw object instead of contextualizing the failure for the user.
- BUG-053 evidence strengthened (3+ open/close cycles + health-badge sampling + latency per-request); BUG-052 reproduction captured with full resolver log chain + raw plugin error + offline transition.
- Cleanup/restore: added a second saved device row (`c64u Unknown · c64u`) for testing, then edited its host field to `192.168.1.13` and Saved & Connect. Final state: `Connected to 192.168.1.13, system healthy`. App foregrounded on Settings. Original `u64 Unknown · u64` row remains (un-selected, harmless).

## Ralph loop iteration #120 (2026-06-18, kilo) — viewport regression root-caused & fixed + build stabilized

- 2026-06-18T09:30:00+01:00 - Startup in `/home/chris/dev/c64/c64commander` on `fix/hardening-4` @ `3fcdf64a`. Dirty tree preserved. Source/installed identity `0.8.8-rc1-3fcdf`.

- 2026-06-18T09:33:00+01:00 - User report: "excessively large area around the device's toolbar. Unused space between toolbar and bottom app viewport about the height of the app's footer. Recent regression, last two weeks."
- 2026-06-18T09:33:00+01:00 - Verified on Pixel 4 with new APK: SCREENSHOT shows TabBar at TOP of a ~330px purple gap, Android nav bar at bottom — clearly a doubled safe-area-bottom in the tab-bar frame.
- 2026-06-18T09:34:00+01:00 - Root cause confirmed via `git show 70492ce7`: `--app-tab-bar-frame-height` changed from `(visual + safe-area-bottom)` to `(visual + nav-padding-y + border + (2 * safe-area-bottom))`. Doubled safe-area-bottom makes frame ~264px taller than needed; visual tab-bar (only `visual + ~10px` tall) sits at TOP of frame, leaving ~143px blank gap below before the safe-area-bottom padding-bottom.
- 2026-06-18T09:35:00+01:00 - Earlier "fix" (padding-bottom dedupe in `.page-shell`) was correct but did NOT address the real issue — the gap is in the tab-bar-frame itself, not the page-shell.
- 2026-06-18T09:36:00+01:00 - Fix applied: `src/index.css:42-43` changed `(2 * var(--app-tab-bar-safe-area-bottom))` to `var(--app-tab-bar-safe-area-bottom)` (single).
- 2026-06-18T09:36:00+01:00 - Test tightened: `tests/unit/pageShellClearance.test.ts:38` added negative regex `expect(css).not.toMatch(/2\s*\*\s*var\(--app-tab-bar-safe-area-bottom\)/);` to lock out the doubling regression.
- 2026-06-18T09:40:00+01:00 - Rebuilt (`./build --skip-tests --install-apk --device-id 9B081FFAZ001WX`); APK `0.8.8-rc1-3fcdf` installed; verified on device — TabBar now sits directly above Android nav bar with no gap. Streams/Config end-of-page screenshot confirms.
- 2026-06-18T09:44:00+01:00 - Stabilize build pass:
